Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Poorly controlled T2DM with high fasting blood glucose and insulin. Stress ECG and lung functions not performed.

Comment Key: SymptomScreeningRecommendation
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Poorly controlled T2DM with high fasting blood glucose and insulin. Stress ECG and lung functions not performed.

Overview Notes: Homocysteine can also increase the risk of heart disease. Supplementing with active B vitamins such as in Phytomulti or a high quality B supplement can help to lower this level.
Comment Key: VitaminsOrSupplements
Comment Value: Multivitamin
Special Investigation Notes: Poorly controlled T2DM with high fasting blood glucose and insulin. Stress ECG and lung functions not performed.
